        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

I have reproduced the issue and found the cause for the crash:



<span class="line"><!---->I have reproduced the issue and found the cause for the crash:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1) In the supplied media_stream2.html file, both the video_type and audio_type are set to DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB. 



<span class="line"><!---->1) In the supplied media_stream2.html file, both the video_type and audio_type are set to DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB. <!----></span>



<br>





2) This results in found_video not being set to true at [1] (since the device.type matches the audio_type),



<span class="line"><!---->2) This results in found_video not being set to true at [1] (since the device.type matches the audio_type),<!----></span>



<br>





3) which then lead to the failed CHECK at [2].



<span class="line"><!---->3) which then lead to the failed CHECK at [2].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/renderer_host/media/media_stream_manager.cc;drc=ab7a15d89d306a247ae4db287b2455e492867c01;l=2499



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/renderer_host/media/media_stream_manager.cc;drc=ab7a15d89d306a247ae4db287b2455e492867c01;l=2499"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/renderer_host/media/media_stream_manager.cc;drc=ab7a15d89d306a247ae4db287b2455e492867c01;l=2499<!----></a>



<br>





[2] 



<span class="line"><!---->[2] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/renderer_host/media/media_stream_manager.cc;drc=ab7a15d89d306a247ae4db287b2455e492867c01;l=2261



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/renderer_host/media/media_stream_manager.cc;drc=ab7a15d89d306a247ae4db287b2455e492867c01;l=2261"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/renderer_host/media/media_stream_manager.cc;drc=ab7a15d89d306a247ae4db287b2455e492867c01;l=2261<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





It seems to me that DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB should not be allowed as audio type, but I am not fully clear on how audio capture is supposed to be specified in this case since there is no audio capture type corresponding to DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB like for the other capture types.



<span class="line"><!---->It seems to me that DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB should not be allowed as audio type, but I am not fully clear on how audio capture is supposed to be specified in this case since there is no audio capture type corresponding to DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB like for the other capture types.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I'll continue with looking into how this issue should be resolved.



<span class="line"><!---->I'll continue with looking into how this issue should be resolved.<!----></span>

You should validate these inputs in media_stream_dispatcher_host and kill the renderer process with bad_message::ReceivedBadMessage() if you get DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB as audio type (or any other invalid input) in the request.



<span class="line"><!---->You should validate these inputs in media_stream_dispatcher_host and kill the renderer process with bad_message::ReceivedBadMessage() if you get DISPLAY_VIDEO_CAPTURE_THIS_TAB as audio type (or any other invalid input) in the request.<!----></span>

<h3 class="medium-heading"><!----> issue</h3>


          


            

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
